League of Nations to Announce: Germany Violated Treaty; Proposed Reply Unacceptable 39

London. According to League of Nations sources, when the League of Nations Council holds a public meeting tomorrow, the representatives will likely unanimously condemn Germany for violating the Locarno Treaty. This matter will be decided at a secret or non-public meeting of the Council tonight. It is rumored that the Council will adjourn after meeting in London tomorrow and will hold its next meeting in Geneva on March 23. (Reuters, 17th)

London. According to the opinions of some delegations in the League of Nations Council, the German reply in its current form seems difficult for the public to accept. The Council must first announce the verdict that Germany violated the Locarno Treaty before discussing Hitler's proposed answer. Germany's request to participate in the meeting on a basis of full equality will make any vote of conviction impossible. It is unreasonable for a country that has violated an international treaty, while other countries are considering its breach of contract, to hope that those countries will discuss its proposed suggestions to replace the treaty it has destroyed. (Reuters, 15th)

London. The German government recently submitted a reply to League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol, accepting in principle the country's participation in the Council meeting, but with two conditions attached. League of Nations Secretariat personnel believe that before the Council holds a public meeting tomorrow afternoon, it should first hold a non-public meeting to study the German reply. British Foreign Office officials also said that the conditions put forward by Germany should be studied by the Council. Its first condition, regarding equal rights, will definitely be opposed by some countries. In the opinion of those countries, the Council should first publicly condemn Germany's act of abandoning the treaty. As for the second condition, that negotiations should begin immediately on Hitler's proposed suggestions, it will also be strongly opposed, because the future decisions of the League of Nations Council cannot be dictated by Germany in advance. According to Hitler's proposals, there are seven points, the main ones being: France, Belgium, and Germany should sign a treaty of non-aggression for a period of 25 years, and the Netherlands can also join; France, Britain, and Germany should sign a treaty on the European and Asian skies; Germany is willing to sign treaties of non-aggression with its eastern neighbors; Germany is prepared to return to the League of Nations, but on the condition that the League of Nations charter excludes the Treaty of Versailles and that equal rights regarding colonies are recognized. (Havas, 15th)

London. According to League of Nations personnel, among the various events related to the situation this week, the issue of sanctions against Germany is the most important. However, at this time, the majority of member states of the League of Nations oppose imposing practical and effective sanctions on Germany. Among them, Britain is deeply afraid that Germany may resort to retaliatory measures in military and financial terms, so it strongly opposes it. Regarding finance, financial circles here believe that once sanctions against Germany are implemented, Germany will definitely abolish the agreement between Britain and Germany on commercial debts. According to the agreement, Germany owes British merchants a total of 15 million pounds, and the repayment method is clearly stipulated in this agreement. British banks rely on this agreement to include German debts under assets. If Germany abolishes the agreement, the debts will have no whereabouts and will naturally be listed as bad debts and written off annually. Then, the banks that maintain the debt will inevitably fall into crisis and have to ask the Bank of England for assistance. As far as the general public knows, the Bank of England strongly disagrees with the sanctions policy and has exerted pressure on the Cabinet to prevent sanctions against Germany. (Havas, 15th)

London. The League of Nations representatives here are increasingly pessimistic about the situation, believing that the severity of the situation is no different from the eve of 1914. Britain hopes that once the League of Nations condemns Germany for violating the Locarno Treaty and the Treaty of Versailles, it should accept Hitler's suggestions and engage in negotiations. However, the demands of the anti-German countries are not only empty condemnations, but also severe actions to follow. The representatives of France, Belgium, Russia, Turkey, and Romania are all demanding sanctions against Germany and hoping that Britain and Italy will assist France. (National Telegraph, 15th)

British Government Disappointed with German Reply; Believes Hitler Aims to Alienate Britain and France 40

Disputes in Manchurian-Mongolian Negotiations: Establishment of Border Affairs Committee 43

The opposition People's Party convened its annual National Representative Congress here yesterday, firmly advocating that in the midst of the current drastic changes in the international situation, Poland's alliance with France must be maintained. Although the party is in opposition, it can represent the masses of farmers in the country, and its advocacy cannot be ignored. In addition, the National Radical Party, which is composed of elements separated from the ruling party, also issued a resolution stating that various organizations formed by people in France are actively operating in Poland, and it is clear that they are directed and subsidized by the German government, but the Polish authorities are actually accommodating them, which is improper. In addition, former Prime Minister and former Army Minister General Sikorski recently published an article in the Polish Post, discussing Germany's re-fortification of the Rhineland, saying that the Rhineland is extremely important to Britain and France in terms of military strategy, and that it is no less so for Germany's eastern neighbors. It also said, "Regarding this incident, the countries concerned are now holding talks in London. From Poland's point of view, regardless of the outcome of these talks, Poland's partnership with France should be made rock solid. The absolute and independent condition for Poland's policy is to advance in the same direction with the current European and French understanding." Former Senator Goscoski also published an article in the newspaper, saying, "Poland has always held a pro-France attitude. This is due to the 'political conscience' of the Polish nation, and not merely out of emotional effect. The position in which France is placed is extremely important for Poland, and Poland’s actions must not be ignored in this regard." (Havas, 15th)

The leader of the "Iron Guard" in Bucharest, the capital of Romania, Prime Minister Goga, recently delivered a speech at a political gathering, saying that since Germany abolished the Locarno Treaty, Romania should cooperate with France, but in his personal opinion, if France and Germany can reach an agreement, it is necessary for Europe to establish lasting peace. As for the agreement between Romania and Soviet Russia on mutual assistance, if Soviet Russia can unconditionally recognize Romania's sovereignty over Bessarabia Province (which belonged to Russia before the war and is now owned by Romania), Romania can sign this agreement. (Havas, 16th)

Clashes Between Left and Right Factions in Spain; Female Party Member Dies by Gunshot 45

Madrid. A civilian who sympathized with the Fascist Party today attempted to assassinate the leader of the Socialist Party and former Minister of Labor, Gabannuro. Madrid. Isogai Convenes Military Attache Conference in Tianjin, Focusing on Public Security and Anti-Communism in North China; Emperor of Japan Sends Nakajima to China to Inspect Troops 78

Tianjin correspondence: Major General Isogai Rensuke, military attache at the Japanese Embassy in Shanghai, along with Major Utsunomiya, military attache, arrived in Tianjin from Beijing on the morning of the 12th. Upon arrival, they were greeted by Staff Officer Doeki and Adjutant Jinbo, dispatched by the Japanese Garrison. They were taken to the Tokiwa Hotel residence, and then went to Zhang Yuan's official residence to meet with Commander Tada. After a discussion lasting about two hours, Tada hosted a banquet. Military attaches stationed in various parts of North China arrived in Tianjin one after another, because Isogai had been ordered to convene a meeting in Tianjin. Those who arrived on the morning of the 12th included Takeashita Yoshiharu, head of the Kwantung Army's Shanhaiguan Special Service Agency, and Hayama Kiro, head of the Suiyuan Special Service Agency. At 2:00 PM that day, Isogai convened a meeting centered around himself within Zhang Yuan's official residence. Attendees included Nagami Toshinori, Chief of Staff of the Tianjin Garrison; Staff Officer Hayashi (Major); Doeki Mitsuo (Captain); Senior Adjutant Otake (Major); Utsunomiya (Major), military attache in Shanghai; Takeashita (Colonel); Hayama (Major), and more than ten others. First, Nagami reported on the recent diplomatic and public security situation in the Hebei-Chahar region. Then, the internal plans brought by Isogai were divided into three points for discussion: 1. The issue of anti-communism in North China, the attitude that Japan should take towards the northward movement of the central army, and the problem of strict monitoring of public security in Hebei, Chahar, Shandong, and Suiyuan; 2. The establishment of the new Hebei-Chahar political power, the attention that should be given to it, and the promotion of its implementation of planned measures; 3. The adoption of close liaison methods among military attaches stationed in China in the future. The meeting lasted a long time, and only ended at 5:00 PM. On the evening of the 12th and the morning of the 13th, Oomoto Shiro, a military liaison officer stationed in Zhangjiakou, and Wachi Takaji, head of the Datong Special Service Agency in Taiyuan, arrived in Tianjin one after another. Isogai convened another meeting to discuss the aforementioned three items in detail. Wachi, a lieutenant colonel, reported on the situation of the communist bandits in Shanxi Province. The meeting adjourned at noon. In the afternoon at 4:00 PM, Isogai, along with Major Utsunomiya and Colonel Takeashita, went to Peiping, where they visited Chairman Song Zheyuan, accompanied by Major Imai, the military attache stationed in Peiping, to discuss public security in North China and exchange views. On the afternoon of the 14th, they left Peiping for Jinan, where they were accompanied by Ishino Shiba, the military attache stationed in Jinan, to meet with Han Fuqu. The trip to Qingdao was cancelled, but Takahashi (Lieutenant Colonel), the military attache stationed in Qingdao, came to Tianjin on the night of the 13th, planning to return to Jinan with Isogai on the 14th in order to discuss everything in the car. Before the 17th, Isogai rushed back to Nanjing to report the results of the consultations in North China to Ambassador Arita. At the same time, Arita will present his views when he visits President Chiang. In summary, the mission of Isogai's trip to North China was mainly focused on anti-communism and public security in North China. The military attache sent by the Emperor of Japan to China was originally scheduled to be attendant Hirayama before the February 26th Incident, but later Major General Nakajima was sent instead. On the morning of the 12th, Nakajima arrived at Tanggu aboard the Great Wall Maru and disembarked. Ishii, a senior staff officer of the Tianjin Japanese military, greeted him. At noon, he inspected the Tanggu garrison, read out the Emperor's message of condolence, and toured the troops' barracks. At 7:30 PM, he took the Beining train to Tianjin, where he was welcomed at the East Station by Tada and his staff, as well as Japanese Consul General Kawagoe. On the 12th, he visited the shrine, inspected the garrison at Haiguang Temple, and read out the message of condolence. In the afternoon, he inspected reservists, the volunteer corps, boy scouts, and the National Defense Women's Association. In the afternoon, he toured military hospitals and various schools. In the evening, he listened to Tada's report on military affairs and Nagami's report on North China's diplomacy and the political situation in Hebei and Chahar at Zhang Yuan's official residence, and attended a banquet hosted by Tada. On the morning of the 14th, he observed the garrison's street fighting exercises. In the afternoon, he went to Peiping to review the troops. On the morning of the 16th, he read out the message of condolence in Peiping. In the afternoon, he went to Tongzhou to comfort the troops and to speak with Yin Rugeng to learn about the situation in eastern Hebei. On the 17th, he flew to Gubeikou to review the troops. In the afternoon, he returned to Peiping. On the 18th, he inspected the topography of the suburbs of Peiping and toured the city. On the 19th, he took the Peiping-Shenyang train through Tianjin to Shanhaiguan to comfort the local troops. On the 21st, he returned to Tianjin, inspecting the troops in Changli, Lulong, and Tangshan along the way. On the morning of the 23rd, he visited Consul General Kawagoe in Tianjin. In the afternoon, he went to Tanggu and returned to his country aboard the Great Wall Maru. (14th)

Xiao Zhenying Holds Birthday Celebration for His Parents; The Celebration Was Prepared for Two Months; The Cost is Estimated at 50,000 to 60,000 Yuan; Tens of Thousands of People Sent Gifts 79

Peiping correspondence: Tianjin Mayor Xiao Zhenying is holding a large celebration this year for his parents' 66th birthday. The celebration preparations began two months ago and were extremely thorough. Recalling the grand birthday celebrations of Zhang Zongchang in the past, this surpasses them. The banquet hall is located in the second courtyard of the residence. There were originally ten trees in the courtyard, but because it was early spring and they had not yet sprouted, the preparation committee ordered florists to cover the trees with peach blossoms made of velvet. Amidst the clusters of flowers, there were also red and green electric lights, which shone brightly at night. In the center of the birthday hall, there was a golden statue of the Old Man of Longevity, with a plaque inscribed by Xu Shichang hanging above. On both sides were couplets written by Yu Youren, Cao Kun, and Feng Yuxiang. Chairman Lin, President Chiang, Deputy Commander Zhang, Finance Minister Kong Xiangxi, as well as Hu Hanmin, Li Zongren, and Bai Chongxi, all sent precious birthday gifts, which were displayed in the corridors, leaving almost no space. Song Zheyuan, Chairman of the Hebei-Chahar Political Affairs Committee, personally wrote a plaque, carved from nanmu, referring to himself as a "nephew." The silver five-piece altar set, publicly gifted by all the officers and soldiers of the 29th Army, was five feet tall, inlaid with green jade, and the craftsmanship of the tripod and censer was exquisite. Division Commanders Feng Zhian, Zhang Zizhong, Liu Ruming, and Zhao Dengyu jointly presented a large silver plaque, with pure gold dragons inlaid around it, which was a noteworthy item for the guests to appreciate.

Although Xiao only sent out three thousand invitations, the number of gift registry entries had already exceeded thirty thousand by noon on the 15th. Some estimate that the value of all the birthday gifts is at least 100,000 yuan. The gifts received on the afternoon of the 15th and the 16th are not included. In addition to the various precious items in the birthday hall mentioned above, there was also a golden slip of paper inscribed with "Mr. Chen Juesheng presents a full banquet from Fengzeyuan." Fengzeyuan is one of the most famous restaurants in Peiping. Xiao's residence has ordered from six restaurants, including Chinese, Western, and vegetarian cuisine. A total of one thousand tables are needed for the two days, and Fengzeyuan alone is responsible for three hundred tables. Therefore, the first to benefit from the grand gathering at Xiao's residence were the gold shops, restaurants, and Xiang embroidery shops, all of which saw their business triple.

On the 15th, for the pre-birthday celebration, because there was a theatrical performance, over a thousand guests arrived by noon. At that time, representatives from the Peiping and Tianjin Chambers of Commerce presented plaques, banners, and umbrellas to the residence, led by a band, with great pomp. Xiao personally came out to welcome them and fired cannons to pay respect. As for other gifts of banners and umbrellas, large and small, there were over a hundred items, filling both large courtyards. After a sumptuous meal, the representatives from the Peiping and Tianjin Chambers of Commerce were invited by Xiao to listen to the opera, including Lu Sujuan's "Qi Shuang Hui" and Shang Xiaoyun's "Han Mingfei." They did not leave until late at night when the performance ended.

The Peiping local authorities, for the security inside and outside Xiao's residence on the 15th and 16th, had carefully agreed on measures with the birthday celebration preparation committee. Police Chief Chen Jiyan and Garrison Commander Shao Wenkai were responsible for security, leading their subordinates to handle matters carefully. At the same time, there were a total of over two hundred greeters from various circles, stationed at the entrance to welcome guests. If the greeters did not recognize a guest, even if they had an invitation, they were not allowed to enter in order to prevent any problems. As a result, many people were turned away. As for the arriving and departing vehicles, designated routes were established. All vehicles entered from the east entrance of the North Barracks Street. After the passengers alighted, the empty vehicles exited from the west entrance and turned north, circling back to the outside of the east entrance of the North Barracks Street to wait for orders. When passengers needed a vehicle, the person in charge would call for it by phone. Military police responsible for maintaining traffic wore special badges for identification.

The 16th was the actual birthday, and the excitement can be imagined. Birthday envoys from various places arrived in an endless stream, from far and wide. There were also those who presented theatrical performances, and famous actors such as Yu Shuyan and Yang Xiaolou performed their best plays to add to the occasion. In short, in the desolate city of Peiping, after the Spring Festival, although thousands of shops had closed down, this grand gathering at Xiao's residence brought a sense of joy to some of the merchants and people who benefited. It is estimated that the cost of the grand gathering at Xiao's residence was at least 50,000 to 60,000 yuan, which is quite impressive. (15th)

Remnant Bandits on the Fujian-Zhejiang Border Gradually Defeated; Gangs Robbing Vehicles on the Fuzhou-Quanzhou Road to be Eradicated Soon; Gao Chengxue's Accomplices Sneak Back to Fuding and are Arrested 80

Fuzhou correspondence: It is reported that remnant bandits have recently been found harassing the Zhejiang border again. The Fourth Pacification Zone Command in eastern Fujian ordered Zhang Qiong, the commander of the 25th Brigade stationed in eastern Fujian, to send troops deep into the area to pursue and suppress them. Xuan Tiewu, the director of the Zhejiang Provincial Security Department, also led the Zhejiang Provincial Security Force to be deployed in the Pingyang and Taishun areas to encircle and attack them. The bandits have been completely defeated. The bandit leader Liu Ying barely escaped with his life. Brigade Commander Zhang has telegraphed the province to report the victory, and Director Xuan has also returned to Hangzhou. In addition, the security regiment is clearing and suppressing bandits in the territory of Fu'an County. The other day, over fifty members of the bandit gang surrendered with their weapons. The regiment has agreed to give them a chance to turn over a new leaf and redeem themselves by meritorious service. As for the areas of Xiapu and Fuding, the Fourth Pacification Zone Command received a telegram yesterday from the First Security Regiment, stating that the Fifth Company of the Second Battalion of the regiment encircled and suppressed scattered bandits in Leibaoluan, killing the leader of the pseudo Third Column Guerrilla Team, Wang Agang, and six other bandits. They seized five rifles, one pistol, and fifty-three bullets. However, Wang Guangchou of Shouning colluded with Zhang Apeng, who seized firearms, and Xu Qiewei to commit widespread pillaging and killing, causing the people to live in misery. Since February of this year, the bandit gang has killed Gong Qisheng and two others in Dashu Village, Ye Jiaxiu and one other in Houkeng Village, Ye Aben and two others in Guanyang Village, Xia Yafang and three others in Zhetou Village, Ye YouShu and four others in Tuanshi Village, Xu Faqian in Tieluping Village, as well as three people in Qiushan Village, eight people in Xidi Village, three people in Badai Village, three people in Caikeng Village, and four people in Danggang Village. However, the surnames are not known.

The bandit gang led by Wei Geng, which robbed long-distance buses on the Fuzhou-Quanzhou Highway, has been surrounded and severely suppressed by government troops. According to military sources, the various units suppressing the bandits are currently attacking from all sides. There have been engagements on the front lines in recent days. The bandits have lost their ability to resist, and some have fled to the islands of Pingtan and Fuqing. In order to eradicate them as soon as possible, the provincial authorities have ordered the Fifth and Tenth Security Regiments and the Fourth Gendarmerie Regiment to actively advance towards the bandits, and have telegraphed the garrisons in Fuqing, Pingtan, Yongtai, Minqing, and Minhou counties to strictly defend and suppress them. It has also been learned that since the robbery case occurred, many bandit parties who fled to various parts of Taiwan have returned to Fujian to engage in activities. Special telegrams have been sent to various coastal units to earnestly investigate and prevent them. The other day, Song, the battalion commander of the Tenth Security Regiment stationed in Gaoshan City, Fuqing County, received a tip that Lin Konghua, a cohort of the Gao Chengxue gang, had led over ten bandits and secretly returned to his residence in Yuanxi. He immediately sent troops to arrest them. The bandit leader Lin Konghua was killed on the spot, and Lin Kongjiang, the brother of the bandit, was captured, along with a rifle. Several other bandits were injured and fled under cover of darkness. Investigations are still ongoing. Yesterday, the provincial authorities dispatched the Special Service Battalion of the Security Department to Fuqing County to reinforce the bandit suppression efforts and temporarily garrisoned in the county seat to suppress the bandits. The 49th Regiment of the 9th Division also dispatched a battalion from Putian to garrison in Honglu Dongzhang in the county to suppress the remnant bandits as the opportunity arose. The county authorities have notified all groups not to be alarmed. The Construction Department also convened the governments and security departments of Minhou, Fuqing, Putian, Xianyou, Hui'an, and Jinjiang counties, as well as the headquarters of the Third and Fourth Pacification Zones, to hold a Fuzhou-Quanzhou Highway Protection Conference in Putian on the 13th to discuss ways to ensure the safety of vehicles on the road in the future.

In northern Fujian, the secret societies in the border areas of Jian'ou, Nanping, and Shunchang counties have been rampant again in recent days, and robberies occur frequently. The other day, the entire family of a certain village head in Baisha, several miles from Yangkou, was seized by bandits. The village head has already been killed. The 56th Division sent a company of troops to investigate in various villages, but the secret societies are extremely cunning. When the troops arrive, they all transform into civilians. When the troops leave, they run rampant in the countryside. The village heads and bailiffs are afraid of retaliation and dare not report, making it impossible for the officers and soldiers to suppress them. Li Yutang, the commander of the Third Division, who has recently been transferred from Pucheng to Nanping, has decided to come to the province in the coming days to discuss the issue of the secret societies in northern Fujian with the authorities. (March 14th)

Noteworthy Doctor in Xiamen, Ye Ruiting, Kidnapped and Murdered; Kidnappers Sent Letter to Victim's Family Demanding Ransom After Murder; Bandits Used Abandoned House as Hideout 81

Xiamen Correspondence: Ye Ruiting, a well-known doctor at Tiande Hall on Datong Road in Xiamen, was kidnapped on March 5th due to his thriving medical practice and accumulated wealth. A group of bandits, calling themselves the "Bird Needle Gang," rented an empty house at No. 77 West Park Road. They sent an old woman with a note to Tiande Hall, requesting Dr. Ye to make a house call. Once he arrived, they abducted him and demanded a ransom of 6,000 yuan, with a five-day deadline, threatening to kill him if the ransom was not paid. They also warned against reporting the incident to the authorities. Police detectives investigated the case for several days without success. Shockingly, on the 10th, Dr. Ye's body was discovered in an empty house at No. 6 Xianfeng Camp, revealing he had already been murdered.

The rented empty house used for kidnapping and concealing the body was not far from the Public Security Bureau. The time between the kidnapping and the discovery of the body was exactly five days. The new houses at No. 6, 8, 10, 12, and 14 Xianfeng Camp are all owned by the Huang family of Cuntang Sixth Market in Junzai Alley. No. 14 was rented to a person named Zai, while the other four remained vacant and were advertised for rent. The keys were left with Zai Jinshan, the tenant at No. 14, so prospective renters could obtain them from Zai to view the properties.

On the afternoon of March 2nd, a young man in his twenties came to Zai to get a key to view a house. They agreed on a monthly rent of 5.5 yuan, and the young man paid a deposit of 5 jiao before leaving. Around 2:00 PM on the afternoon of March 5th, the same young man returned for the key, saying he was going to clean up the place in preparation for moving in. Several days passed, but he neither returned the key nor moved in. Upon inspection, the door had been replaced with a new lock. Zai reported this to the landlord, Huang Shangjin, who together with Zai hired a locksmith to open the door. Inside, they found an empty box, a pair of black trousers, a hemp rope, a wad of cotton with traces of blood, apparently used to gag someone, and a cloth bag. In the back room, there was a pile of earth and sand, a broom, and two rows of floor tiles, with ten tiles already loose, as if they had been pried up and relaid. Realizing something was amiss, they reported it to the Second Branch of the Public Security Bureau.

Workers were hired to dig beneath the loose tiles, and after digging two feet, they found a human hand. Continuing to dig to four feet, they unearthed a corpse. Someone recognized it as Ye Ruiting and immediately telegraphed Ye's family and the court. Ye's family arrived and confirmed the identity of the deceased as Ye Ruiting. The court examined the body and found the limbs not yet stiff. The deceased was wearing a black cloth short shirt and pants, black socks, and cloth shoes. There was a wound on the forehead, the skin slightly broken, about an inch long, without any damage to the bone, appearing as a graze. Blood had flowed from the ears and nose, and blood had also flowed from the anus. The jawbone was protruding, the skin unbroken, but the inner bone was protruding. There were rope marks on both wrists, forming a diagonal pattern, with a purplish-blood color. The entire body showed black and blue bruises. The left eye was tightly closed, while the right eye was slightly open. It was determined that the deceased had been buried alive and suffocated. However, the time of death could not be determined. After the examination, the court instructed Ye's family to prepare the body for burial.

After Ye was kidnapped, his family and employees were threatened by the bandits and kept the matter secret. When detectives heard rumors and inquired, they were still hesitant to reveal everything. They had also followed the bandits' instructions and replied to a letter, nailing it to a utility pole on West Park Road, requesting a reduction in the ransom. The letter was indeed taken, but there was no further response. On the morning the body was discovered, they received another letter from the bandits, stating: "Our gang initially borrowed 6,000 yuan, which had to be paid within five days. Now that the deadline has passed and you have not paid the full amount, and you have reported the case to the authorities, which is truly abominable. Now that the deadline has passed, 10,000 yuan is required. If you delay any further, we will take drastic measures."

It seems that the bandits who kidnapped Ye were well-organized and had a detailed plan. The empty house at No. 77 West Park Road and the empty house at No. 6 Xianfeng Camp, where Ye's body was hidden, were both rented on March 2nd. On the afternoon of March 5th, Ye was kidnapped on West Park Road. On the same afternoon at 2:00 PM (one hour before the kidnapping), they had already picked up the key to No. 6 Xianfeng Camp. According to neighbors of Xianfeng Camp, they saw people carrying a wooden box into the house on the evening of the 5th, assuming it was movers and did not pay attention. However, some said they first saw them carrying it in on the 9th. It is difficult to determine when exactly it was carried in.

The box, upon inspection, was 2.5 feet deep, 3 feet long, and 2 feet wide. It was a wooden box used to store orchid-brand tobacco. The box had luggage tags from a hostel that said "28 Nihonmachi, Old Pasar, Singapore, Yuanji Hostel" and "Xu Tianxu Ershun" and "Fujian." It appeared to be the belongings of someone returning from Southeast Asia. There were two footprints inside the box, as if Ye had struggled violently inside after being bound. The broken skin on the head was likely caused by hitting the box during the struggle. The fox-fur coat, worth 200 gold yuan, which Ye was wearing when he was kidnapped, had been stripped off. Ye's body and the surrounding area were covered in a great amount of white powder that resembled lime. When smelled, it had a medicinal odor, likely used to absorb the moisture from the decaying body to prevent swelling and odor. The meticulousness of the planning and the composure of the actions are evident. Even after Ye's death, they sent a letter demanding a ransom, seemingly wanting to hide the body and then extort another sum of money. Therefore, some suspect that in addition to the kidnapping for ransom, there may have been underlying resentment. This can only be proven after the case is solved.

Furthermore, Wu Ruifu, a famous doctor on Kaiyuan Road, received a letter on the 12th signed "Bird Needle Gang" demanding money. The letter stated: "We kidnapped Ye Ruiting and incurred significant expenses, resulting in financial difficulties. Please quickly send 3,000 yuan to Miaoshi Temple, where our gang will send someone to collect it. Otherwise, we will take drastic measures against you." It is unknown whether this was done by the kidnappers of Ye or someone else using their name to intimidate Wu. (March 15th)

Songjiang: Resignation of Members of the East Yong'an Fire Brigade

The East Yong'an Fire Brigade in the second district of this city has recently been greatly inconvenienced in firefighting due to a lack of hoses. It was proposed to purchase ten new ones, requiring 500 yuan. A meeting of the board of directors was convened to discuss fundraising methods. However, none of the nine directors attended. The members, feeling disheartened, jointly submitted their resignations to the leader on the 16th.

Caojing Police Station Apprehends Long-Time Bandit

Niu Wanpi, an officer from the ninth substation of the Public Security Bureau, learned that Feng Jindou, also known as Zi Gen, from No. 6, Jia, Sipao, Chongque Three Bao, was suspected of being a bandit. He immediately dispatched a team to arrest him. Under interrogation, Feng confessed to robbing Chen Baogen's house in Sunjiaqiao, the Xia family and Gan Mingsi's house in Yinglong Township, and Feng Zhaolin's house in the Sixteenth Tu, among others. All of these robberies occurred in December of last year, one after another. The Public Security Bureau has copied the confessions and sent them to the county for investigation and prosecution.

Suzhou: Car Accident Causes Death

Xu Mao Yuan, the 18-year-old son of Xu Jinshou, a villager from the Ninth Tu, Yidu, Hengtang Township, six or seven li from the city, and an apprentice stonemason in Huangshanhong, was walking on the Sumu Highway near Xikuatang on the 15th when a long-distance bus No. 4 from Sumu Road, traveling from Suzhou to Mu, swerved to avoid another small car, knocking Xu Mao Yuan down. He suffered severe injuries to his abdomen and legs, and bled profusely, losing consciousness. At the same time, Qiu Da Xiaomao was also injured. The bus immediately stopped and transported the injured to the city, intending to take them to Bo Xiong Hospital for treatment. Xu Mao Yuan died in the vehicle due to the severity of his injuries. Qiu Da Xiaomao was sent to the hospital for treatment, and it is believed that his life is not in danger. The driver, Ling Jiangsheng, was detained by the Third Branch of the Public Security Bureau and reported to the District Procuratorate for dispatch of personnel for inspection. The Third Branch of the Public Security Bureau sent Ling Jiangsheng to the Public Security Bureau for transfer to the District Court for interrogation on the 16th. All expenses for the coffin and burial of the deceased are to be borne by the Su-Fu Long-Distance Bus Company. The company will also convene a board of directors meeting to discuss compensation issues.

Social Education Personnel from Various Counties Submit Petition to the Ministry for Relief

Social education institutions in counties such as Su, Xi, Chang, and Kun have been ordered to shut down, and closed on the 15th. The social education personnel will go to the province for training to prepare them for future roles as principals of central primary schools and guidance of civic training matters. However, the social education personnel are concerned that salaries will not be paid during the training period, and they are opposed to this. After a discussion at the Education Association of Wuxi County previously, on the 16th, the social education personnel of each county jointly submitted a petition to the Jiangsu Provincial Government and the Department of Education, requesting that salaries be paid during the training period to maintain their livelihoods, and also submitted a petition to the Ministry of Education for relief.

Wuxi: Buddhist Monk of Juesheng Temple Taken to Court

Ying Ru, the abbot of Juesheng Temple in Huishan, was reported to the Supervisory Section of the Public Security Bureau in July of last year by a visiting monk, Zhi Lun, for harboring filth. Police were dispatched, broke into the underground chamber, and found smoking paraphernalia, bamboo tiles, women's clothing, shoes, and other items. The monks Ying Ru, Zhi Yin, and Chang He, as well as a woman named Jiang Wenzhen (also known as Miss Jin), were taken to the bureau and transferred to the county government for detention. The county government sent Ying Ru and others to the County Rehabilitation Center for compulsory drug rehabilitation, and later sentenced them to imprisonment. They have now completed their terms. However, the monks are also suspected of digging up graves, which should be handled by the judiciary. Yesterday, the county government transferred them to the court. After an interrogation by Prosecutor Lu, he ordered that they all be detained pending investigation.

District Secretaries Across the County Appeal

The county government had already abolished the fee charged by district secretaries for issuing certificates. An order was issued to each district to strictly prohibit this. Upon learning this, the district secretaries of each tu and district were greatly alarmed, believing that their livelihood was in jeopardy. The district secretaries convened a meeting on the premises of the Chengqu Primary School on Sanhuang Street in the city to discuss relief measures. More than 400 district secretaries from across the county attended the meeting. They decided to elect representatives to petition the Party and government authorities, unanimously appealing that if they do not receive satisfaction, they will all resign.

Actively Constructing the Wuxi-Xi Highway

Since the completion of the Wu-Jiao Highway, there has been no highway between Wujin and Wuxi. Previously, the Wu-Jiao Long-Distance Bus Company proposed the construction of the Wu-Xi Highway and submitted a plan and budget to the Department of Construction for approval. After receiving the submission, the Department of Construction believed that the construction of the Wu-Xi Highway was necessary, but the project was massive and difficult to begin immediately. Currently, the Department of Construction plans to send personnel to Wuxi within a few days to survey the route. The road will start from Henglin in Wu, passing through Lishe, Yuqi, Qianzhou, Beiqifang, and Shichuang, to Tangtou Bridge, connecting to the Xi-Cheng Highway, and reaching Wuxi. Another theory is that the road will start from Henglin and reach Qingyang in Jiangyin, connecting to the Xi-Cheng Highway.

Changzhou: Civil Servants Undertake Labor Service

Civil servants in the urban area of Wuyi County are undertaking labor service to construct the ring road around the city. The county government has ordered technician Shen Zhiyu to set the central markers, and work began on March 15th. At 8:00 AM that morning, all county government employees gathered in the grand auditorium for roll call, then proceeded to the Third Section to collect hoes and other tools before departing for the construction site outside the South Gate. More than 1,000 employees from other agencies also arrived on time to start working, displaying great spirit and diligence, and did not disperse until the evening. It is also reported that the construction projects of the county government and the county Party headquarters have been completed, while other agencies and schools will continue to work on the 16th.

Zhenjiang: Eight County Treasuries to be Established

In order to standardize the revenue and expenditure of local funds in counties of Jiangsu Province, the provincial government established county treasuries. Since its establishment, it has had great success. Currently, with the exception of Jiangpu, Jurong, Lishui, Yangzhong, Pixian, Siyang, Xiaoxian, and Yizheng, all other counties have already established them. It is reported that the provincial government has decided to establish treasuries in the eight counties of Jiangpu, etc., and will order the Farmers Bank and the Jiangsu Bank to establish offices or branch offices in four counties each. It is understood that the Farmers Bank has decided to establish offices in Jurong, Jiangpu, Lishui, and Yangzhong, and has appointed Chen Yanxiang, Gu Shixiang, Hua Yaxiong, and others to be responsible for the preparations. The Jiangsu Bank will establish offices in Yizheng, Qixian, Xiaoxian, and Siyang and has also appointed people to prepare for their establishment. Currently, they are actively working on it and will be completed soon.

Nantong: County Magistrate Hong Takes Office

The newly appointed Nantong County Magistrate Hong Sheng (courtesy name Zhuangyou, from Liaoning) arrived in Tong from Shanghai on the 15th and took office on the 16th. The former county magistrate, Jin Zonghua, has left Tong. The handover was handled by his secretary. The key officials of the county government are appointed as follows: Secretary Tian Honghai, Chief of the First Section Wang Youwen, Chief of the Second Section Zhang Yu, Chief of the Third Section Wang Mengzhou.

Yangzhou: Ten-Year-Old Boy Dies in Bicycle Accident

The ten-year-old son of Lu Ganling (American), the principal of the American-Chinese Middle School of the Anglican Church inside the Bianyi Gate in Yangzhou City, was intelligent, lively, and loved by all. He was particularly skilled at riding bicycles and was beloved by his father. During leisure time, father and son often went to the suburbs together, riding bicycles for pleasure. However, this morning (15th) at 10:00 AM, Lu went to school for worship. The child tried to ride his father's bicycle. Because the bike was high and his legs were short, he fell from the bike as soon as he left the gate. He was stabbed in the left eye by the iron bar of the bicycle. He was found and helped up by a gatekeeper but was already unconscious. Lu rushed back, called for a doctor to diagnose and treat him, but he bled too much and died before treatment could be administered.

National Studies Specialization School Opens

The National Studies Specialization School in Yangzhou held its opening ceremony this morning (15th) at 9:00 AM. More than 30 students and dozens of representatives from various agencies and groups attended. Hu Zhen and Han Guojun (represented by Ma Shuang) and Wang Boling, were elected as permanent directors of the school board, with Wang Boling presiding over the ceremony. Wang reported on the preparations. Next, Zhou, the principal of the provincial middle school, and Xin, the director of the Education Bureau, gave speeches, saying that the school was training talents for the future, with unlimited prospects. Then, Jiang Taihua, the principal of the school, responded, and the group took pictures before the meeting adjourned. It is reported that the school's curriculum includes Classics (taught by Xu Xibo), Prose and Parallel Prose (taught by Chen Ciqing and Cheng Xizhi), Poetry (taught by Cheng Cangguang), and History and Geography (taught by Jiang Wuzi and Zhang Yuping).

Dinghai: Second Section of the Dinghai Fire Brigade

The various districts of Dinghai City are densely populated and commercially prosperous. However, firefighting equipment is still primitive. A proposal was initiated in the 22nd year [of the Republic] to organize and establish a fire brigade, which has now been in existence for four years, with remarkable achievements. To facilitate firefighting, a second branch association is being established at the foot of Dongyue Temple Mountain. Zhou Xiangsheng, a gentleman from Dinghai who lives in Shanghai, donated funds to build the association hall, which has now been completed. The opening ceremony is scheduled for April 1st.

Bengbu: Human-Powered Rickshaw Donation Trend Expands

Regarding the issue of rickshaw pullers requesting a reduction in donations, the provincial government has clearly ordered a reduction of two jiao, with payment of one yuan. The rickshaw pullers belonging to the rubber-tired rickshaw association have complied and received licenses. Most of the rickshaw pullers from the rickshaw pullers' union are still waiting. On the 14th, three hundred rickshaw pullers gathered at the Rickshaw Pullers' Union to discuss how to respond. They split into two groups, one going to the Public Security Bureau to petition, and the other going to Dama Road, where they destroyed the rubber-tired rickshaws that had already received new licenses. The police on duty stepped forward to stop them, but were attacked by the rickshaw pullers, and three policemen were injured and a pistol was lost. Two rickshaw pullers were beaten. The situation was very chaotic for a time and the situation was very serious. Upon receiving the report, the Public Security Bureau immediately dispatched a large number of police officers to suppress them, dispersing the petitioning rickshaw pullers and arresting twelve rioting rickshaw pullers. One soldier who had mixed in and caused trouble and two women, relatives of the rickshaw pullers who went to the bureau to cause trouble, were also taken to the bureau and detained for interrogation. Thirty-seven rickshaws belonging to the rubber-tired rickshaw association were destroyed and towed to the bureau for inspection. The Public Security Bureau immediately convened an emergency meeting with the military, police, Party, industrial, and commercial agencies. It was decided that: 1. The rickshaw puller riot should be reported to the provincial government and the provincial Party headquarters by the Public Security Bureau, the Party headquarters, and local organizations. 2. The damaged vehicles of the rubber-tired rickshaw association will be temporarily repaired by the Public Security Bureau on behalf of them. 3. The Military and Police Supervisory Department will issue a notice to strictly prevent riots. 4. The riot incident will be resolved by representatives from the labor union, the rickshaw pullers' union, the military and police agencies. 5. A thorough investigation will be conducted into the attack on the police on duty and the theft of a pistol, and the perpetrators will be severely punished according to law.

Letter to the Editor 82

Dear Editor,

I am writing in response to an article in the "Outlying Areas Correspondence" section of your newspaper on the 15th of this month, concerning Sun Lu Qiangfen, the wife of Sun Zhonghao from Shintangwan, Wuxi. The article stated that Lu Qiangfen was the daughter of Lu Mingshu, the owner of the Luyoufeng Soy Sauce Garden on Guanqian Street in Wuxi, and a former teacher at Tangwan Elementary School in Shanghai. I am greatly surprised.

Lu Qiangfen's family had already published a notice in the Shen Bao and Min Bao on November 18th of last year, severing the father-daughter and family relationship because of misconduct. As for the suggestion that she was a former teacher at Tangwan Elementary School, many teachers have left Tangwan Elementary School, and it is unfair to generalize. Furthermore, Lu Qiangfen's misconduct occurred after she left the school and is a matter of personal morality, having absolutely nothing to do with the school. Moreover, there is no graduate named Chen Lin.

Therefore, I am writing to inform you and respectfully request that you promptly make a correction. I would be most grateful.

Sincerely,

Lu Yunqian, Principal of Tangwan Elementary School, Shanghai

March 15th

Han-Guangdong Travelogue (6) (Travel Correspondence from Our Newspaper Reporter) Hengyang 83

— Zhao Junhao

The Yuehan Railway spans 1,096 kilometers, running from Guangdong to Hankou, with Hengyang as its central point. Consequently, the Zhushao section of the Engineering Bureau is located there. This area is a major county in southern Hunan, densely populated with bustling markets. Numerous scenic spots and historical sites are scattered throughout. With the full completion of the Yuehan Railway, the importance of Hengyang's position is self-evident.

We traveled from the foot of Mount Heng to the outskirts of Hengyang by car along the highway to the car station. Originally, we could have disembarked here, but since the car could enter the city, we drove into the city. The city walls are exceptionally low, easily reached by hand. The car drove in, and the archway almost reached the top of the car. The city is bustling and well-organized, and diligently promotes a new way of life, with signs directing pedestrians to keep to the left in the middle of the road. The road is being widened, with houses being demolished on both sides, but the road surface has not yet been completed. It is said that the Hengyang County government plans to use the revenue from fertilizer taxes to fund the road construction, which could generate tens of thousands of gold dollars a year. The commerce in Hengyang can be compared to that of Wuxi. Large stores are mostly located on the west bank of the Xiang River, in the Fencheng area. Branches of the Shanghai Bank, the Bank of China, and the Commercial Press are located there.

The Zhushao Section Engineering Bureau is located on the east bank of the river. It took us no more than five minutes to cross the Xiang River to reach it. After landing, the entire construction resembled a new urban area, with wide roads and rows of streetlights. At the crossroads, there were new-style police booths, round or square, extremely beautiful. The booths were also illuminated with red lights to facilitate traffic. We took a rickshaw from the riverside, and after ten minutes, we saw a magnificent building, which was the newly built Hengyang Station. This kind of architecture is still rare in southern Hunan. According to the Ministry of Railways' plan, it was originally intended to build the Engineering Bureau's office in Hengyang. However, the bureau, considering the short construction period, believed that there was no need to build it to save expenses. The Ministry of Railways approved the early construction of the station, and the bureau was relocated there before the railway was completed, to facilitate office work. Hengyang Station is a second-class station. The exterior architecture adopts a simple, dignified, modern three-dimensional style, divided into three levels: the underground level, the ground level, and the upper level, with dozens of rooms, all practical. Currently, passenger trains from Hengzhou run to Chenzhou, and many passengers enter and exit the station daily.

In addition to the station building, the bureau also allocated a large area south of the station as a residential area for its employees, covering more than 50 acres, with 16 buildings, divided into three Type A buildings, four Type B buildings, eight Type C buildings, and one apartment building. Each building has a square in front, planted with flowers and trees. Electric lights and running water are readily available. The residential area is called Lizhi Li, which resembles the new-style Shanghai alleys. However, these residences are all bungalows. Ding Wenjiang contracted coal poisoning in Hengyang, which was in the guesthouse in Lizhi Li. Hengyang is bitterly cold, making it unbearable. Spring is still like this, let alone in the depths of winter. Ding's coal poisoning was initially saved, but his old illness relapsed, leading to his death. Alas!

Mount Heng boasts many scenic spots and historical sites, including Huoyan Peak, the first of the 72 peaks of Mount Heng. It is said that geese fly here and turn back, hence the name. Also, the Dongzhou Bamboo Forest, with its secluded bamboo-lined paths, is where Wang Chuanshan taught. A Chuanshan School has been established nearby to commemorate him. In addition, when Wu Sangui fled to Yunnan, he first opened the altar here, so Hengyang still has the name Donghua Gate, and there are still traces to be found. In addition to those mentioned above, there are also Shigu Mountain (i.e., Shigu Academy), Yueping Mountain, Huayao Temple, West Lake, Sidu Pavilion, and Jiashuyuan (i.e., the Zhushao Section nursery). Due to time constraints, we were unable to visit any of these.

Hengyang is not only the central point of the Yuehan Railway, but also has highways that connect to Guangxi. Currently, the highways in Hunan Province have been built to the border, but the highways in Guangxi have not yet been extended due to the many high mountains along the route, making construction difficult.

When the employees of the Zhushao Bureau first came to Hengyang, due to the large number of people, they mostly purchased supplies from the markets, so the local area gained some income. However, prices inevitably rose over time. In fact, with so many employees, it would have been possible to set up a consumer cooperative when they first arrived in Hengyang, so that supply and demand could be met, and life could have been more comfortable.

Recently, in order to expedite the completion of the Yuehan Railway, the Ministry of Railways has sent three supervising commissioners to the railway. They are Zhou Liangqin, the chief engineer, Xia Quanshou, the chief engineer, and Nie Zhaoling, the section chief of the New Railway Construction Committee. Chief Engineer Zhou is old and served in the surveying department in the early days of the Yuehan Railway. In 1932, he served as the chief engineer of the Shaoguan-Lechang section. He knows the history of the railway well. Chief Engineer Xia also inspected and accepted the Shaoye section of the project. Section Chief Nie was the director engineer of the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway. These three are highly respected in the engineering field. After arriving, they visited the various engineering sections and made many plans for the progress of the railway project.

Minister of Railways Zhang Gongquan will inspect the Yuehan Railway. All parties are preparing to welcome him in the coming days. Li Xiangen, the director of the Southern Section, and Li Luchao, the director of the Guangzhou-Kowloon Railway Bureau, will both go to Hengyang to meet him. It is said that a comprehensive plan for the reorganization of the Southern Section and the Hubei-Hunan Section will be decided after the inspection.

Local News

Bank Acceptance House Established Yesterday; Committee Sets up Guarantee Evaluation and Management Groups; Acceptance Date Should Not Exceed Ninety Days 84

The Shanghai Bank Acceptance House was officially established yesterday morning and began operations. All member banks may enter into an acceptance contract with the house. A committee and two groups, Evaluation and Management, have been set up to handle the related affairs. Details are as follows.

Bank Acceptance House Established Officially Yesterday Started Operations

The official establishment was announced yesterday morning. The address is at the United Bank Preparatory Committee, 59 Hong Kong Road. The manager is Zhu Boquan and the deputy manager is Xu Baoqi. There was no ceremony. Any bank that has joined the acceptance house may enter into an acceptance contract with the house and submit the types of collateral specified in the articles of association. If the review is passed, the acceptance will be granted. However, the due date of the accepted bill, calculated from the date of issue, may not exceed ninety days. The handling fee is 0.25 per mille of the face value for every ten days, as the minimum amount.

Committee Established to Preside Over Business

The first chairman of the Acceptance House is Zhu Boquan, the permanent committee members are Cheng Muhao, Li Muyi, Tong Chengdao, Zhusen Sheng, and Yin Jiyuan, and the committee members are Zhang Naiqi, Chen Sensheng, Zhuang Jingwu, Zhou Jiyun, Zhang Zhuyu, and Zhang Jinglu, a total of twelve people. The term of office is one year and can be re-elected. They handle the acceptance affairs of the Acceptance House bills. The decision has been made to expand once the business has been effective.

Evaluation and Management, Two Groups of Committee Members

The Acceptance House Committee has established: a Collateral Evaluation Group, headed by Yin Jiyuan, with committee members Shi Jiqing, Zhang Jinglu, Zhuang Jingwu, and Tu Luqin; a Collateral Management Group, headed by Zhusen Sheng, with committee members Tong Chengdao, Zhang Zhuyu, Wang Zhenfang, and Liu Tong. The types of collateral stipulated are various major domestic products, domestic commercial bills of exchange and promissory notes for foreign payment, government bonds and stocks with market prices, real estate in this city, and other goods and properties approved by the Executive Committee of the Association.

Municipal Finance Bureau and Land Bureau Director Xu Fu Assumed Office Yesterday Morning; Xu Discussed Streamlining Finances with Both Revenue Generation and Cost Reduction; Announced Slight Changes to Secretaries and Section Chiefs of the Two Bureaus 85

Mr. Cai Zengji, the director of the Municipal Finance Bureau and acting director of the Land Bureau, resigned. Upon the recommendation of the Municipal Government, the central government appointed Mr. Xu Fu to succeed him. Mr. Xu arrived at the bureau around 9:00 AM on the 16th to assume his duties. The details of his assumption of duties are recorded as follows:

Meeting of the New and Former Directors

Former Director Cai Zengji arrived at the bureau at 9:00 AM to prepare the handover procedures. The new Director Xu Fu also arrived at the bureau at 9:30 AM. The two directors met in the Finance Bureau Director's office, had a brief discussion, and then began the handover. After the weekly memorial service at 10:00 AM, Director Cai left, and the new director personally escorted him to the gate.

Congratulations from All Sectors

After Director Xu arrived, friends of Mr. Xu came to offer their congratulations. For a time, the traffic on Fenglin Bridge was like shuttles. Those who came included Yu Zuoting, Chairman of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce; Cai Jingjun, Director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau; Bao Guohua, Deputy Manager of the Municipal Bank; Zhu Runsheng of the Farmers Bank; Zhu Dazhai, Manager of the Municipal Bank; Lu Bingnan, Assistant Manager of the Xingye Trust Company; Wang Yansong, member of the Municipal Party Headquarters; Yang Hu, Director of the Security Office; Fu Xiaoan of the Tonghua Bank; and Jin Tingsun, Le Junbao, and over a hundred others.

Speeches by Cai and Xu

At 10:00 AM, the Finance and Land Bureaus held a joint weekly memorial service in the Finance Bureau. Both the former and new directors attended. After performing the rituals, former Director Cai Zengji delivered an introductory speech, stating that he had resigned due to being appointed General Manager of the China Merchants Bureau by the central government and was unable to handle both positions. He added that the Municipal Government had appointed Director Xu to succeed him and that everyone should strive harder in the future, under Director Xu's guidance, to further improve the city's finances and land administration. Subsequently, new Director Xu Fu delivered a speech, stating that he had been appointed director of the Finance and Land Bureaus, and that all administrative policies would follow the established practices. He hoped that everyone would continue to serve diligently and work as hard as they had in the past to ensure that the bureau's affairs progressed smoothly. After Director Xu's speech, the meeting adjourned.

Announcement of Secretaries and Section Chiefs

After Director Xu assumed office, the official announcement of the secretaries and section chiefs of the two bureaus was as follows: Chen Zhongjiu and Gao Hanqiao, secretaries of the Finance Bureau; Chen Jun, head of the First Section (reappointed); Shi Lei, head of the Second Section; Xia Maoxin, head of the Third Section; Yang Nianzu, head of the First Section of the Land Bureau; Lu Dachi, head of the Second Section (reappointed); Fan Yongzeng, head of the Third Section (reappointed); Yu Mengshao, head of the Fourth Section. There were no other changes to the staff.

Announcement of Assuming Office

Xu issued an announcement stating: "According to the Shanghai Municipal Government Order No. 1214, I have been appointed Director of the Finance Bureau. In addition to submitting a report, I am ordered to assume office as soon as possible. Upon receiving this order, I assumed office on the 16th of this month. In addition to reporting this separately, I hereby announce it for general knowledge."

Xu Discusses Revenue Generation and Cost Reduction

According to Xu's statement to the Central News Agency reporter, he had been appointed director of the Finance Bureau and acting director of the Land Bureau, and that everything would follow established practices. As for streamlining the city's finances, it would involve both revenue generation and cost reduction, and he would continue to follow Mayor Wu's intentions to promote the development of the two bureaus' operations.

Postponed Swearing-In Ceremony

Xu originally planned to hold a swearing-in ceremony at today's Municipal Government weekly memorial service, but it was postponed because Mayor Wu was ill and on leave. The date for the postponed swearing-in ceremony will be decided after the mayor recovers.

Central Savings Society Opened Yesterday Morning 86

Finance Minister Kong Xiangxi Delivered a Speech; Supervisory Committee Members Took Office and Held Their First Meeting

The Central Savings Society opened yesterday morning. The members of the Supervisory Committee were sworn in and held their first meeting. Standing committee members were elected. Finance Minister Kong Xiangxi attended in person and delivered a speech. The details are as follows:

Guest List

Those who went to congratulate the society yesterday morning included Xu Kan, Zou Lin, Bei Songsun, Shi Jiu'ao, Qi Yunqing, Hu Xi'an, Mu Ouchu, Zhao Jinqing, Yuan Ludeng, Lu Jianquan, Jin Guobao, Song Ziliang, Yan Xifan, Xu Weizhen, Zhu Boquan, Wang Yansong, Zhang Shouyong, Zhou Jue, Chun Junzhuang, Zhu Runsheng, Yu Zuoting, Xiao Xianguang, Wang Zhixin, Fang Jiaobo, Zou Bingwen, Xu Jiqing, Yang Jemei, Huang Boqiao, Wu Shaozeng, Xi Demao, Hu Meian, Lin Kanghou, Ye Fuxiao, Dai Mingli, Fu Xiaoan, Zhang Weiru, Liu Hongsheng, Hu Bijang, Cai Jingjun, Chen Jintao, Zhou Zongliang, Wang Baolun, Wang Boyuan, Wei Jingzhou, Wu Yunqi, Qian Xinzhi, Xu Xinliu, Li Shuxiong, Pan Gongbi, Wang Yingbao, Li Denghui, and over a thousand others.

Supervisory Committee Members Took Office

Supervisory Committee members Chen Jian'an, Li Fuxun, Ning Hanzhang, Xiao Lai, Qin Runqing, Du Yuesheng, Qian Xinzhi, Yu Qiaqing, Guo Shun, Chen Guangfu (absent), Guo Bingwen (absent) and others held a swearing-in ceremony at the society at 11:00 AM yesterday morning and held their first meeting. Chairman Kong Xiangxi, as well as directors Ye Zhuotang, Xu Kan, and Song Ziliang, were present. After each supervisory committee member was sworn in, the meeting began. Chen Guangfu was elected chairman of the Supervisory Committee, and Li Fuxun and Chen Jian'an were elected standing committee members. During Chen Guangfu's absence abroad, Li Fuxun will act as chairman. Qin Runqing, Wang Xiaolai, and Yu Qiaqing were also elected to supervise the lottery drawing at the first lottery. The committee's rules of procedure were then discussed, and the meeting adjourned at 11:30 AM.

Opening Ceremony

The Party and national flags were hung high at the entrance of the Central Savings Society on Hankou Road. The auditorium was located on the second floor of the society, in the meeting room. A portrait of Sun Yat-sen hung in the center, with the Party and national flags crossed on either side. A vase of fresh flowers sat on the podium, and flower baskets from various sectors were placed around the room. Guests signed their names downstairs and were given copies of the Central Savings Society's charter and membership application forms. Manager Li Shuming, Deputy Managers Zhu Shikang and Zhang Xisan, and all staff members greeted the guests. The opening ceremony began at 11:40 AM. Guests and all staff members attended. Finance Minister Kong delivered a speech, and the ceremony adjourned at 12:00 PM.

Kong's Speech

At 11:40 AM, Finance Minister and Director Kong Xiangxi gathered all staff members in the main auditorium and delivered a speech. Director Ye Zhuotang reported, "Today is the opening day of the Central Savings Society, which has been specially approved by the government. Please, Minister Kong, deliver a speech." Kong then delivered a speech, saying, "Fellow colleagues, today is the opening of our Central Savings Society. Saving is a virtue. From youth to old age, people initially rely on their parents, and when they are able to stand on their own, they support their families. Moreover, our country is a family-oriented society. In addition to supporting their wives and children, people also support their parents. However, when they are old and weak, they should retire. At that time, they should have a way to support themselves. In the past, they relied on their children to support them in their old age. Now, social ideas are changing, and they cannot completely rely on their children. They should save their surplus during their working years to use for retirement. Our country has 400 million people. If each person saves one yuan, they can accumulate 400 million yuan. For example, the water of the Yangtze River flows from the upper reaches. The source of this water is the melting snow on the mountains or the accumulated rainwater. Therefore, collecting sand can form a tower, and accumulating small amounts can become a large amount. However, the money that is accumulated should be deposited in a reliable savings institution. At the same time, the savings institution can use the savings to develop agriculture, industry, and commerce. In the past, there was no reliable institution. Now, banks such as the Four Banks have a joint organization to expand their strength. Regarding national savings as a whole, the government has entrusted the Central Trust Bureau to establish the Central Savings Society to achieve the goal of benefiting the country and enriching the people. When the Central Trust Bureau opened, I encouraged my colleagues with the words 'trust' and 'effort.' Today, the opening of the Central Savings Society has many meanings. It is to cultivate the virtue of national savings. At the same time, it is to use the people's savings to regulate the social economy. The purpose of the lottery savings is to encourage people's hope for savings. Everyone should work hard and uphold the principle of 'trustworthy,' so that the savings business will prosper. Use small savings to develop the country's entire agricultural, industrial, and commercial sectors. Today, we are honored to have leaders and representatives from all sectors to guide us. I would like to express my gratitude."

Enthusiastic Savers

From 9:00 AM yesterday, many people went to the Central Savings Society to obtain the charter. Because the society has preferential savings methods, over a thousand households have already joined. At the same time, many depositors of the Sino-French Savings Society went to the society to apply for exchanging their slips to continue saving.

National Postal Workers' General Union Held Its Third National Congress Yesterday; Passed Many Important Proposals; Sent Telegram of Condolences to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek; —Five Groups Jointly Held a Banquet Tonight— 87

According to Dagon News, the Third National Congress of the National Postal Workers' General Union held its opening ceremony and preliminary meeting the day before yesterday. Yesterday morning, it held its first official meeting, and in the afternoon, it continued to hold its second meeting. It passed many important proposals and sent a telegram of condolences to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek. The details are as follows:

First Meeting

Yesterday morning at 9:00 AM, the union held its first official meeting in the hall on the fourth floor of the Ningbo Fellow Villagers Association on Xizang Road. Sixty-five delegates and nine observers attended. Zhu Xuefan presided over the meeting, and Kong Fanzao served as the recorder. As it was Monday, the weekly memorial service for Sun Yat-sen was held. After the rituals, the chairman reported that today was the first official meeting of the congress, and it was auspicious to hold it on the anniversary of Sun Yat-sen's death. We must follow Sun Yat-sen's past spirit of struggle and work hard to promote the union's work and create a glorious history of the postal workers' movement. After the memorial service, the formal meeting began. First, Secretary-General Zhao Shusheng reported, followed by the receipt of many congratulatory telegrams. Representatives from Yunnan and Nanning were unable to attend due to the distance and time constraints. The presidium decided to appoint alternate representatives Shen Jizhou and Liu Xinquan from Shanghai to represent Yunnan, and alternate representatives Xia Junrui and Song Shilin from Nanjing to represent Nanning, effective immediately. Li Liqiang, a comrade from the Hankou Postal Workers' Union, was suspended for his efforts in union affairs, and he came from Qingdao to participate. The presidium approved his attendance to show their appreciation. According to the union's regulations, all observers from local postal workers' unions must be approved by the presidium. The presidium approved the attendance of Li Liqiang, Zheng Wenquan, Hong Yongzhi, Chen Jingbao, Lin Guozhen, Chen Defeng, Zhu Xiangming, Ye Yunhan, and Li Anhe. The presidium decided that due to limited seating, only union officials were allowed to attend.

Work Report

After Secretary-General Zhao's report, a representative of the outgoing executive committee made the following work report: (A) General affairs: The outgoing executive committee held three joint meetings of the executive and supervisory committees, one meeting of the executive committee, and twenty-four meetings of the executive committee's standing committee. It received 1,344 documents and sent 1,470 documents. The financial report is detailed in a separate written report. (B) Organization: There are currently 45 unions. Those that are being reorganized or restored are the unions in Xi'an, Dihua, Wuchang, Shashi, Chongqing, Beiping, Zhangjiakou, Guihua, Baoding, Taiyuan, and various unions in the four northeastern provinces. (C) Propaganda: The "China Postal Worker Monthly" has been published to the third issue of the second volume. (D) A brief overview of important union affairs. Finally, he hoped that the congress delegates would review the general report and express sincere condolences to the delegates and executive committee members from various places for their efforts in supporting the union.

Discussion of Proposals

After the report, the discussion of proposals began. According to the presidium's agenda, the morning session discussed proposals from the union affairs group, and the afternoon session continued to hold the second meeting to discuss proposals from the bureau affairs group. A total of 37 proposals were submitted by the union affairs group. After review, five were deemed unnecessary to be submitted, five were to be submitted to the presidium, and seventeen were to be submitted to the congress for discussion. Many important proposals were resolved.

Condolences to Chiang Kai-shek

The first resolution was the proposal on how the union should express its condolences to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek for his hard work for the country. It was decided to send a telegram of condolences in the name of the congress. The text of the telegram is as follows: "To Chairman Chiang Kai-shek of the Military Affairs Commission, since you have led the revolution, you have been diligently training the army and striving to be diligent. Your achievements are widely praised. At a time when the country is in deep crisis and the nation is in danger, we rely on your wisdom to guide us, to establish the foundation for the nation's new life, and to shoulder the great responsibility of revitalizing the nation. We, the representatives of the entire congress, respectfully lead 38,000 postal workers across the country with the utmost sincerity, to show our extreme resonance, and to serve you. We send this telegram of condolences. The entire delegation of the Third National Congress of the National Postal Workers' General Union, Lu Jingshi, Wang Yisheng, Han Dayong, Zhang Guangdai, Zhu Xuefan, and 72 others."

Other Important Cases

Other important resolutions included determining the general outline of work during the extraordinary period, designating February 1, the date when the union's preparatory committee began working, as Postal Workers' Movement Memorial Day, expediting the handling of pending cases from previous years, implementing them as soon as possible, and other important cases. In the afternoon, the second meeting was held to discuss proposals from the Bureau Affairs Group (the contents will not be published due to the need for further editing).

Nominate Delegates

The association yesterday also passed a resolution to nominate delegates to petition in Beijing to request the central government to promulgate postal workers' union organizational laws and regulations. Twenty-one delegates were nominated to petition in Beijing, and their names are as follows: Li Shaoyu, Lu Jingshi, Zhu Xuefan, Wang Yisheng, Cao Jiaxiu, Sun Dakun, Zheng Tingjie, Zhang Yidao, Zhang Guangdai, Han Dayong, Cheng Zuoqing, Jiang Shuli, Huang Zhaoguang, Chen Shigao, Zhao Shusheng, Zhao Yanqi, Mao Yongnian, Yang Yuli, Lou Qicheng, Ge Lianfang, Wei Desen.

Party Banquet

The Municipal Party Headquarters held a banquet for postal worker delegates from various regions at the Atlantic Hotel last night at 7:00 PM. Wu Kaixian, Tong Xingbai, Jiang Huaisu, Lu Jingshi, and over one hundred delegates attended. During the banquet, Jiang Huaisu gave a welcoming speech, and Chen Tugao gave a thank you speech. The guests and hosts enjoyed themselves and dispersed at 9:00 PM. Tonight, the International Labor Bureau, the China Industrial Federation, the Municipal Federation of Trade Unions, the China Labor Association, the Ningbo Fellow Villagers Association, and five other groups will jointly host a banquet at the Atlantic Hotel.

Continued Review

The association received over 500 proposals from various regions. The four review committees worked through the night the day before yesterday, but they have not yet completed the review. The review committee will continue to review last night in order to submit them for discussion at the third and fourth meetings today.

Common Interest, Concession Board of Directors Set to Elect Western Directors on Schedule 89

The election of Western Directors of the Board of Directors of the Public Concession will be held on the 23rd and 24th of this month (Monday and Tuesday). There are two polling places: one in the drill hall of the Shanghai Volunteer Corps of the Board of Directors, and one in the Hongkou Police Station. The time will be from 10:00 AM to 3:00 PM. The election tickets will not be issued in advance. Any citizen with the right to vote can go to one of the above locations at any time to receive the election ticket. At that time, the Motor Transport Section of the Police Department will also have regulations on the arrival and departure of vehicles. In order to avoid crowding, foreign citizens will be asked to vote early.

Westerners Carry the Board of Directors, Glimpses of Councilmen's Election, Westerners Hope to Vote, Japanese Bridge Denies Seeking Control 90

According to the Great American Evening News, this year's councilman election of the Board of Directors, because the Japanese have nominated three candidates, one more than usual, is expected to be the most intense election in the history of the Shanghai Public Concession. If all three Japanese candidates are elected, it will not only overturn the distribution system of foreign councilmen of the Board of Directors for many years, but the total number of Asian councilmen will exceed the total number of non-Asian councilmen. At present, the councilmen of the Board of Directors are two Japanese, five Chinese, five British, and two Americans. If the Japanese occupy three seats, then China and Japan will have a total of eight seats, while Britain and the United States will have a total of only six seats. The Japanese Election Committee is currently conducting a large-scale election campaign. The American Election Committee met with Mr. He Weishi, Secretary of the American Chamber of Commerce, this afternoon (17th) to discuss ways to encourage Americans to vote. This morning, Mr. Peiersheng, the person in charge of the British Election Committee, claimed that the committee is currently doing its best to ensure that the five British candidates and the two American candidates win the election. According to statistics, there are 864 Japanese citizens in Shanghai with the qualifications to vote, 1,350 British citizens, 400 American citizens, 200 German citizens, and 1,000 citizens of other nationalities. The attitude of the German citizens is now very important. According to statistics, the total number of votes cast in previous years was the highest in 1934, with a total of 1,787 votes, of which the Japanese cast 800 votes. It is not possible to predict how many votes the Westerners will cast this year. However, if 850 Japanese people come out to vote, then there is a possibility of winning. However, if non-Japanese voters pay attention to this election and vote for British and American candidates, they can also reverse the situation. The Japanese Election Association yesterday denied the claim that the Japanese are trying to control the Board of Directors.
