Local Martial Arts Groups Express Opinions on Tai Chi Exercises for Participation in the World Games, to be Adopted by the World Games Preparatory Committee and Used to Train Participating Athletes 172

The upcoming World Games will commence on August 1st in Germany. Our nation is actively preparing to participate. Recently, members from the local Martial Arts Hall and various martial arts groups believe that Tai Chi exercises have value in representing our country and performing in Germany at the World Games. Therefore, they have drafted a written opinion and submitted it to the World Games Preparatory Committee for consideration. Our reporter has obtained the original text of the opinion, which is as follows: In recent newspapers, the schedule of the World Games was published, commencing with the opening ceremony on August 1st and concluding with the closing ceremony on the 16th. The daily programs include athletics, swimming, various ball games, weightlifting, wrestling, fencing, martial arts, shooting, sailing, rowing, cycling, and equestrian events. Additionally, German and Swedish-style gymnastics are included. The nature of the World Games is an exhibition of sporting achievements. The venue should gather interesting, valuable, and historically significant materials related to physical education, to provide appreciation and adoption for the audience, and to demonstrate the comprehensiveness and soundness of the Games themselves. The purpose of the World Games to collect all kinds of sports as much as possible is none other than this. The sports mentioned above all occupy a considerable place in the history of physical education, and among them, the gymnastics category should attract our attention. Gymnastics is the most easily popularized sport in physical education, and it is listed as a formal course in schools. Therefore, all countries in the East and West regard gymnastics as a basic sport. Although the competitive element it contains is not as strong or interesting as other competitive sports, its great effectiveness surpasses all sports. The World Games will stage various gymnastics performances for the world, allowing physical education experts from various countries to critique and adopt what type of gymnastics is most suitable for physiology and can serve as a model for modern gymnastics. The profound intention and the importance attached to gymnastics can be seen here. Gymnastics is best known for the German and Swedish styles, which have long been adopted by countries around the world. However, in recent years, the Tai Chi exercises invented by Dr. Chu Minyi of our country, according to researchers, are actually superior to the German and Swedish styles in terms of effectiveness and value. Its excellent performance in last year's National Games was witnessed by the audience. To make readers understand its advantages, a brief description is provided below: Tai Chi exercises are based on the principles of Tai Chi Quan. Its circular movements allow all joints of the body to move simultaneously, and all parts of the body and mind develop equally. It also adopts the characteristics of ordinary gymnastics routines, making the movements gradually deepen from the upper limbs to the lower limbs, the head, waist, and torso, progressing in an orderly manner and coordinating by system. With more interest, memorization is easy. It also incorporates physiological and psychological elements, integrates and connects them to form this exercise. Therefore, when practitioners use it, they can make the intention reach the mind, the spirit follow it, enliven the body and mind, and make the hands and feet agile. The stretching of the whole body joints and the smooth flow of blood circulation have particularly special effects. Our country's physical education community has such a new invention. It should contribute the research results to the all-encompassing world sports exhibition. Not only can valuable criticisms and promotions be obtained in academics, but also the shame of the "sick man of East Asia" can be washed away due to the effectiveness of the Chinese-style gymnastics invention. It is hoped that the members of the preparatory committee for the World Games will adhere to the main purpose of promoting sports regardless of boundaries, promote the spirit of fearing to be behind in academic development, pay considerable attention, and adopt our contributions. Using the most economical and convenient method, part or all of the athletes participating in the upcoming events can be trained in Tai Chi exercises for a short period of time one month before going abroad, so that Chinese-style gymnastics can also be performed in the World Games arena, refreshing the audience. This is what we earnestly hope for.

The South China lineup is as follows: Fei Shaojun, Zhou Shenxian, Wang Qi, Shen Fuqing, Wen Yichen, Jin Fengde, Meng Wenbin, Wu Shuping, Xiao Wenbin, Lu Maoqing, Zheng Shilin, Yao Guofan, Zhang Xiaoyuan, Zhu Chunrong, Li Dehua, Yang Chunlin.

Letter from the Chinese Vocational School Little Ball Team 176

To the esteemed Editor,

In your newspaper the other day, in an article about the Pudong Little Ball team, you stated that our team member Yao Guanfan bought the top of Wang Degen. After reading this, we couldn't help but burst out laughing. The so-called Yao Guanfan and Wang Degen are actually the same person. He changed his name to Wang Degen to participate in the competition due to various family reasons (this does not violate the association's charter). At the time of registration, he had his own photo, which is kept in the association for verification (after the recent game, Mr. Huang verified the photo and found no error). Now that the association sees that our team is about to win the championship, it does not hesitate to reverse black and white and make such a ridiculous move. Our team's participation in the competition is merely an amateur game, and we have no selfish intentions regarding gains or losses. If the association must give the championship to its favorite, it may as well say so clearly, and our team is willing to hand it over to please the association. Now that the association promotes sports on the one hand and infringes on the legal rights of others on the other, which is so absurd, it is a departure from the normal state of promoting sports. We say to the association that right and wrong will eventually be clear, and it is impossible to cover up the truth from the world with one hand.

Chinese Vocational School Little Ball Team, March 16th.

Recently, the existing goods, closed-shop goods, and silver shop mortgage goods stored in Eastern and Western firms have all been traded in large quantities. In addition to the current seasonal medium-thick serge, flannel, and flannel, Melton thick woolen cloth, which is needed for autumn and winter sales, has also been traded. It is also heard that the new goods of Melton thick woolen cloth arriving in Shanghai this winter will be priced about 40% higher than the old ones.

Shenbao Medical and Pharmaceutical Supplement

The Nursing Profession in China Today (Part 1) 194

— Li Lingdong

The nursing profession today is a modern and emerging profession. In advanced countries in Europe and America, the nursing profession is recognized as a basic profession that protects the health of the nation and serves society. It has a close and critical relationship with the strength of the country and the progress of society. It occupies a significant practical need in the entire social group. Therefore, the promotion of the nursing profession and the development of nursing education are progressing rapidly.

Looking back at the situation of the nursing profession in our country, it has a history of more than 50 years. Why is it that the government authorities and people from all walks of life still cannot understand the importance of the work of the nursing profession and the inevitability of the existence of the nursing profession? Furthermore, can the medical and pharmaceutical community, which is closely related to the nursing profession like limbs, correctly and deeply understand the true meaning of the nursing profession? I am afraid that it is very rare. Then, in the social groups of other countries, the nursing profession can be regarded as important, but why is it behind in the Chinese social environment of the same country? This is indeed the most urgent central issue that the nursing profession needs to study at present. Therefore, we must think and observe a lot to see what the current situation of the Chinese nursing profession is, so as to provide basic reference for promoting the nursing profession in the future. A. The General Situation of the Nursing Profession

(1) The Administration of Nursing Schools Cannot Be Independent. The backwardness of the nursing profession in China can be attributed to many complex problems. However, the most important crux that prevents the nursing profession in China from developing and progressing is the lack of independence of the nursing schools themselves, the unsound organization, and the control of the administrative power by the hospital authorities. The budget of a school, the selection of teaching talents, the compilation of curriculum and teaching materials, the equipment of books and instruments, and all kinds of equipment must be built on a solid school administrative organization. Undoubtedly, the issue of the independence of the administrative power of the nursing school is the central mechanism that controls the success or failure, rise or fall of the nursing profession. However, the number of nursing schools established in China is indeed not small, and they have seemingly established the banner of school independence. In reality, the administrative power of the school is entirely manipulated, controlled, and dominated by the hospital. Since the school administration is managed and controlled by the hospital, what is the value of the existence of this puppet-like school? This is nothing more than wanting to use the name of the school to attract and confuse the public, so as to recruit male and female students, and work as the most economical and basic laborers in the hospital. Therefore, it is more pleasing to say that it is an administrative organ for hospitals to recruit laborers than to say that it is the existence of the school itself.

(2) The Decline of Nursing Education. Since the school administration cannot be independent, all the facilities of the school are of course lacking. It is very obvious to us that we cannot talk about the possibility of nursing education at all. Establishing the central goal of nursing education and laying the foundation for teaching principles cannot be considered as the nursing education has gone to the road of decline, and it is becoming more and more acute day by day. Since the whole purpose of recruiting students is not to cultivate talents and to be suitable for the needs of society, but to save hospital costs as a prerequisite, in terms of "teaching," the knowledge of nurses, the skills of nursing, can only take into account the current needs of the hospital as the scope, and cannot consider the conditions to adapt to the society in the future. In terms of "education," it does not take the psychological needs of students and the state of mind as the standard of "education," but instead establishes strict rules and regulations, and three chapters of the law, so that students spend the whole day in an unorganized and unsystematic apprentice-style life. Under the current situation of nursing education where teaching is not education and education is impossible, it can be considered that the period of decline of nursing education has come to an end. (To be continued)

Resurrection (Part 2) 195

— Yueqi

—Eighteenth Medical Story—

One day, a white-haired old man was sent to the hospital. He was very ill, and as soon as he entered the hospital, he underwent surgery. Two weeks later, he underwent a second operation. As soon as the anesthetic was administered, the old man stopped breathing and his heart stopped working. Artificial respiration could not save his life. So the surgeons decided to perform the final treatment. They prepared a liquid containing one part per thousand Epinephrine. Five minutes after the old man collapsed, the liquid was injected into his left ventricle. The effect was very rapid. Within thirty seconds, the old man began to breathe, and his heart began to beat again.

Since then, such miracles have become commonplace. Countless lives have been saved by this method. Some collapsed during surgery, some were stillborn infants, and some died from electric shock. Currently, this method has been practically applied in hospitals.

One day, in the area of Di Tuo Lio, a thief was killed by the police. He was clearly dead and sent to the hospital. After being injected with epinephrine, he woke up, although only for a short time, but enough to give the names of his accomplices.

However, in none of these cases could doctors determine that the resurrected person was truly "dead." This is not surprising, because no one can determine when the human body actually dies. The so-called "sudden death" seems to be non-existent.

Sometimes it is assumed that the end of life is sudden, like flipping a switch to cut off the current. In fact, the rule of "death" is slow, gradual, and similar to the collapse of a great empire. The brain and heart are like the capital of the empire, dying first. The cells of other parts of the body, like the colonies of the empire, are not immediately extinguished, but wait for the final collapse. Without nourishment sent from the capital, without reinforcements to help kill the "enemy"—harmful chemical changes and bacteria—they finally die.

Therefore, it is difficult to determine the moment of the transition between "life" and "death." Common tests, because they do not include the procedure of "cutting open blood vessels," are not completely reliable. The cessation of breathing and the cessation of heartbeat, although often accompanied by "death," cannot always be regarded as evidence of "death."

"Apparent death" is common. Recently, in a London park, a child was seen on the ground, his body cold, with no pulse, obviously dead. After being sent to the hospital, the doctor also confirmed that he was dead and issued a death certificate. As the body was carried to the cemetery, ready to be buried, the child's mother arrived. She heard others say that her son was dead, and firmly refused to admit it; she presented three death certificates previously issued by doctors for her child, and everyone was surprised to wait. After a while, the child woke up and walked home with his mother.

Even perfectly healthy people can sometimes feign death. At an exhibition in Lahore, India, there was a case of a living person feigning death. A mendicant named Harodas voluntarily fainted. He was placed in a bag in a wooden box and buried in the soil ten feet above the ground. There were sentries guarding the ground, and there was obviously no fraud or trickery. After forty days, the soil was dug up, and the monk's body was brought into the air. Before long, he actually sat up and asked for food.

Since the determination of "true death" is so difficult, the "resurrection" that Dr. Connersey is working on is undoubtedly a question of whether it can truly be realized. However, thanks to the progress of medicine, the fate of "unjust death" and "early burial" can at least be avoided.

World View of Tuberculosis Statistics (Part 1) 196

— Ding Huikang

If we want to prevent the occurrence of a disease, we must not only study its causes, but also pay attention to its spread, historical changes, and human geographical relationships. This is what statistics is all about. This science of statistics has recently become a necessary tool for any scientific research. In the United Kingdom, it is regarded as one of the most important subjects in public health. For example, Wolff proved that the number of deaths due to tuberculosis in the industrial areas of European countries has gradually decreased due to the gradual improvement of their sanitation facilities. Wolff also proved at the same time that there is a relationship between tuberculosis mortality and cancer mortality and housing, and found that there is a direct relationship between tuberculosis mortality and residential density, while there is none in cancer mortality.

Taking the tuberculosis mortality statistics of Germany as an example, from 1924 (the year when Germany collected disease mortality statistics throughout the country) to 1932, there were obvious changes as follows:

The number of people who died of tuberculosis per 10,000 residents

1924 12.0 1925 10.7

1926 9.8

1927 9.3

1928 8.8

1929 8.7 1930 7.9

1931 7.9

1932 7.5

From the above statistics, the number of deaths per 10,000 residents decreased from 12 to 7.5. This achievement shows the efforts of anti-tuberculosis efforts over the years. In 1930, there was a slight pause in the decrease in the number of deaths. According to Flatzeck Holbauer, this pause in the decline is due to cultural and sanitary relations, and more importantly, to economic relations. Frantz believes that most patients belong to the poor class, but after the improvement of sanitary facilities, the death rate of tuberculosis is also reduced.

Frantz believes that the reduction in tuberculosis mortality can be observed in two ways and periods. The first period was from 1885 to 1925. During this period, there was a real reduction in tuberculosis mortality. Since 1925, it has been the second period. The reason for the reduction in mortality is due to the progress of nuclear therapy and the development of anti-tuberculosis work.

Goldstein's statistical opinion is that from the standpoint of public health, the reduction of tuberculosis mortality is extremely related to occupation and nutrition, and less related to housing. The organizations of public clinics and insurance institutions are directly related to the reduction of tuberculosis mortality.

According to Jckert's research, it is believed that at present, Germany has no major problems with the nutrition of the people due to the organization of public protection and the progress of public health. Even if there are people with insufficient nutrition, they will not individually affect the tuberculosis mortality rate. However, if malnutrition affects other issues, such as clinics and anti-tuberculosis work, work regulations, housing levels, industrial areas, etc., it is related to tuberculosis mortality.

Hofbauer believes that the poor have a considerable correlation with the occurrence of tuberculosis.

Neumann believes that the reduction of tuberculosis mortality in Germany and Austria is illusory and not a real reduction. Looking at the declining situation over the years, the annual reduction is somewhat, almost with a certain regularity, and how is it so procedural, which makes people question. This gradual reduction in mortality may be due to the fact that after the World War and the famine, tuberculosis initially increased and then gradually decreased. However, in 1921, the tuberculosis mortality rate in Germany was the same as before the war. In any case, the risk of tuberculosis infection has been greatly reduced compared to before, so the mortality rate has also decreased.

According to Ascher's research, the reason for the reduction in tuberculosis mortality is the reduction in people's working hours.

Page 16

Less, increasing mechanical capacity, and the maintenance of human physical strength. In addition, the direct relationship is that work and rest must be scheduled, and the human body increases its resistance as a result.

Wolff and Gundel believe that the reason for the reduction of tuberculosis mortality is due to public health on the one hand, and genetic relations and the progress of medical treatment on the other hand. Considerable achievements have been made in civilized countries. However, the economic situation of German society in recent years is not very good, but the tuberculosis mortality rate has been reduced more than in other countries. There must be special reasons, and the strict organization of public health insurance is undoubtedly the reason. Because other countries do not have such a health insurance organization method. Looking at Geissler's research over the years, it was found that the mortality rate of tuberculosis is lower among working employees, and the mortality rate of those in free professions or leadership professions is higher, which is particularly noteworthy.

Looking at the tuberculosis mortality rate in various parts of Germany, there are slightly different points. The lowest is Hessen, with 5.11 deaths per 10,000 people due to pulmonary tuberculosis, Sachsen is 5.7, Baden is 6.0, Bayern is 6.4, and Preussen is 6.46. Hessen is an agricultural area, and Sachsen is an industrial area with a denser population.

Domestic Medicinal Plants (Continued) 197

— Zhou Mengbai

(22) Dandelion Taraxacum Platycarpum, Dahlst

(Botany) Grows naturally in the mountains and fields. It is a perennial herb. The leaves emerge from the roots, lanceolate in shape, with large serrated lobes. The lobes are triangular with tooth-like edges and sharp tips. In spring, it blooms with head-shaped flowers, the ligulate flowers being yellow. The fruit is small and slender, spindle-shaped, with a pappus of fine white hairs.

European dandelion T. Officinale, Web. grows naturally in Europe and America and is slightly larger than the previous species. The tip of the head-shaped flower involucre has no bony protrusions.

White-flowered dandelion T. Albidun, Dahlst. grows naturally in the central and southern parts of Japan and has white flowers.

(Crude Drug) Dandelion Radix Taraxaci Cum Herba refers to the previously mentioned plant, its roots collected and dried before flowering. The product is spindle-shaped, with short, fine fibrous roots, measuring 0.5-2.5 cm in diameter and 10-20 cm in length. The surface is grayish-brown, with longitudinal deep grooves and wrinkles. The fractured surface is flat. It tastes neither sweet nor bitter.

(Ingredients) The composition of this species has not yet been studied. The components contained in the roots of the European dandelion have been identified, as shown below.

Acetic acid, 3-4-cinnamic acid, palmitic acid, cerotinic acid, oleic acid, linoleic acid, Taraxasterol C29 H24OH, Homotaraxasterol C25 H39 OH, Cluytianol C29 H46O(OH)4, Cholin, etc.

(Medicinal Use) Dandelion is mainly made into dandelion juice (dandelion extract), used as an antipyretic, hemostatic, sudorific, stomachic, and tonic, but this is no longer common. It is also said to have the effect of promoting bile secretion.

Dandelion extract, 0.5-2.0 cm each time, several times a day, used as pills or aqueous solutions.

Prescription example: Dandelion decoction, effective in promoting breast milk secretion.

Dandelion 6.0 Dang Gui (Angelica sinensis) 4.0 Shuyu (Dioscorea japonica) 2.0 Xiangfuzi (Cyperus rotundus) 2.0 Mudanpi (Paeonia suffruticosa) 1.0 The above is made into a decoction of 200cc, taken three times a day.

Folk remedies: When breast milk secretion is insufficient, soaking dandelion leaves and taking them several times a day is effective. In Germany, dandelion roots are chopped, roasted, and used as a substitute for coffee.

Common Knowledge Q&A on Teeth (24) 198

— Lin Jianxian

Section 3: Adult Oral Hygiene

(Question 117) Why is it that most people brush their teeth improperly?

Answer: The main purpose of brushing teeth is to clean the mouth and remove food debris. Most people brush horizontally from side to side. With this method, the bristles cannot easily reach the gaps and convexities between teeth. Food hidden there cannot be completely brushed away. Moreover, if the toothbrush is stiff, horizontal brushing easily causes the gums at the neck of the teeth to recede, exposing the root. Because the root is softer, prolonged friction erodes it into small grooves, which is harmful.

(Question 118) What is the proper way to brush teeth?

Answer: You should brush vertically up and down, that is, brush the upper teeth downwards and the lower teeth upwards along the tooth gaps. This makes it easier to brush out the food stuck in the gaps. Then, brush horizontally a few times to remove any remaining debris. Another method that can also be used is to brush in a circular motion. At this time, do not open your mouth too wide, and brush both the upper and lower teeth at the same time. This method combines both vertical and horizontal movements and is easy to perform. You can choose either of the above two methods.

(Question 119) What other points should be noted when brushing teeth?

Answer: There are three other points to note:

(1) The inner side of the teeth, that is, the side near the tongue, must also be brushed. If vertical brushing is inconvenient, horizontal brushing can be used. (2) The occlusal surface of the molars is prone to cavities, so it should be brushed more to remove food debris. (3) The last teeth inside the upper and lower cavities must also be brushed.

(Question 120) Besides the teeth, what other parts should be brushed?

Answer: The second purpose of brushing teeth is to strengthen the gums. Therefore, when brushing teeth, the inner and outer gums should be brushed, whether horizontally or vertically. In addition, the surface of the tongue should also be lightly brushed a few times. In the morning, this is especially important to remove accumulated debris.

(Question 121) How many times a day should you brush your teeth?

Answer: Once in the morning and once after each meal, for a total of four times a day. Brushing after dinner is the most important because food in the mouth ferments and becomes acidic more easily at night than during the day. Therefore, you should brush more thoroughly before going to bed. Also, you should brush immediately after each meal. If you eat food again after brushing your teeth after dinner, you should brush your teeth again.

(Question 122) What kind of toothbrush should you choose?

Answer: The toothbrush should not be straight because our teeth are arranged in a horseshoe-shaped curve. Therefore, the surface of the toothbrush should also be curved so that it can be conveniently and closely fitted when brushing. The bristles of the toothbrush should not be too hard or too soft. Too hard can easily damage the gums and cause bleeding; too soft will not remove dirt. The bristles in the middle of the toothbrush should be staggered like canine teeth and should not be flat like a cut. They should also be arranged sparsely and not too densely. If they are too dense, the water will not dry easily, and bacteria will easily multiply. Currently, there are two types of toothbrushes on the market with a crescent-shaped concave and convex surface. The concave one is used to brush the outside of the teeth, and the convex one is used to brush the inside of the teeth. You should buy both and use them at the same time, which is more convenient and beneficial when brushing.

Common Knowledge of Hygiene for Ear, Nose, Throat, and Eye Diseases 199

— Tang Renjin

(81) Diphtheritic Conjunctivitis

Diphtheria is commonly known as white throat. It occurs most often in the pharynx and larynx. It occurs less often in the nasal cavity. These three types of diphtheria conditions have already been published in this column. What is described now is a type of diphtheria that occurs in the conjunctiva of the eye. This type of conjunctivitis is often secondarily infected by the diphtheria bacteria. Its main symptom is that initially the eyelids become red and swollen. Then, a grayish-white pseudomembrane develops on the conjunctival surface of the eyelids. The pseudomembrane is formed by the coagulation of fibrin contained in the eye secretions. It appears as a dirty grayish-white color. Its hardness is very strong, and it is not easily peeled off. If forced to peel off, it can bleed. This is a characteristic feature of general diphtheria pseudomembranes. If the pseudomembrane deeply invades the conjunctival tissue, it can compress the blood vessels and cause tissue necrosis. The necrotic conjunctival tissue can often fall off together with the pseudomembrane, resulting in ulcers. Therefore, after the disease is cured, the conjunctival surface often leaves scars.

Complications of diphtheritic conjunctivitis are often corneal ulcers and corneal perforation. These complications are more likely to occur when combined with streptococci. The inflammatory symptoms of conjunctivitis are also more severe. Therefore, its prognosis is generally poor.

This disease must be distinguished from other pseudomembranous conjunctivitis. Because conjunctivitis caused by streptococci, staphylococci, pneumococci, and gonococci, etc., can sometimes develop grayish-white pseudomembranes on the conjunctival surface of the eyelids. At this time, bacterial examination can easily distinguish them.

If the disease has been definitively diagnosed, a large dose of diphtheria antitoxin should be injected early, which is often effective. At the same time, treat the affected eye. If the affected eye is only on one side, then protective goggles should be used to protect the healthy eye on the other side to prevent infection. This is of utmost importance.

Essays

Cannonballs and Workers' Housing 200

— Li Wen

German leader Hitler, in his speech to the people in Karlsruhe regarding the dispatch of troops to the Rhineland area, said: "Currently, a twelve-inch cannonball costs three thousand marks. With an additional fifteen hundred marks, I can build a worker's house. Firing a million of these cannonballs is of no benefit, but their value can build countless workers' houses." This is Hitler's "peace" speech. He declared to the world with great satisfaction: "Today's Germany is truly the most 'peaceful' country in the world." In ancient China, there was the event of calling a deer a horse. The "peace" that Mr. Hitler speaks of is probably similar to this.

However, Mr. Hitler's statement that a twelve-inch cannonball plus fifteen hundred marks can build a worker's house is very meaningful. Analyzing why countries around the world must have extremely strong military forces, sparing no expense of half of each country's financial resources to build terrible and cruel killing machines, what is the reason for this? On the one hand, we see that in countries around the world, there are hundreds of thousands of hungry masses, their voices hoarse, their blood and tears flowing, writhing under the oppression of hunger and cold, unable to maintain even the mere right to "live." What is the reason for this? If the current military equipment of countries around the world, and the money used to build this massive military equipment, were distributed, what would the world become? Currently, the military expenditure of countries around the world often accounts for 30% to 40% or more (such as Japan) of their total expenditure. Building an airplane costs tens of thousands of dollars, and building a warship costs millions or even tens of millions of dollars. Manufacturing a twelve-inch cannonball costs three thousand marks, which is still a very small expense. However, on the other hand, the finances of various countries are constantly announcing the increase in "deficit," and the people's taxes are being increased as much as possible. In a few countries with a small amount of "worker insurance," this insurance is eventually canceled or further reduced. The original purpose of human labor was to seek a better and more comfortable life, but now the whole world is using its strength to do the work of exterminating humanity. Is this the normal path of human history? Or has the whole world gone astray?

Mr. Hitler said very nicely that manufacturing a twelve-inch cannonball costs three thousand marks, plus fifteen hundred marks, "I can build a worker's house." But the cause he is actually pursuing is precisely to exhaust himself in manufacturing twelve-inch cannonballs.

Two Soldiers in Manzhouli 201

— Chen Ji

At dusk, Manzhouli was as silent as if it had died, immersed in desolation. Only the dogs barked and ran, making one feel a little alive. - However, what a sad vitality!

Two men, called "devil soldiers," walked shoulder to shoulder, stepping disorderly, chattering about something they themselves did not understand. They stared at the desolate front, walking disorderly.

"Look! Our motherland is over there!" The taller one pointed to the distant front.

The shorter one nodded with silent worry, expressing his sincere reply.

Then everyone was chattering in a mess again. Suddenly, the shorter one sighed and said:

"Let's not think about our home anymore!"

Silence. The wind in Manzhouli at dusk blew on people's faces, so cold that the whole body felt like it was falling into an ice cellar. However, the two soldiers seemed not to feel it at all, and walked aimlessly forward.

They walked into a village, full of dilapidated walls and crumbling walls, and a kind of desolate sorrow also seeped into the hearts of the two soldiers. They looked at each other, and then their steps faltered.

Just at this moment, suddenly in front of their eyes, like a ghost, a small animal slipped past their eyes. Perhaps the small animal was frightened, but she ran to the two soldiers. The taller one picked her up. The child cried:

"Mom - Mom - oh!"

"Don't cry! No..." He said, struggling to speak the local dialect. He looked at her little face. "Ah!... Look!" He turned his head to the shorter one. He couldn't help but hug her tightly and deeply kiss her little face.

The child cried loudly.

But he said to her in a trembling voice: "No, no, don't cry! Little sister! Where is your father? Where is your mother?"

The little girl glanced at him with frightened eyes. Seeing that he had no malicious intent, she trembled and replied: "Father and mother were killed by you!"

Hearing this, the two soldiers were shocked as if struck by lightning. They looked at each other again. At this time, they only heard a voice like tearing paper crying out: "Give me back my granddaughter! Give me back - " An old woman cried to them: "You killed my children, my daughters-in-law, my,... Do you still want to kill my child?" The old woman couldn't say anymore, just crying.

They returned the little girl to the old woman and left in a hurry.

The next day at dusk, the two soldiers appeared here again. They each carried a few packages of things. They found the little girl's house. The taller one held the child in his arms and put a few packages in front of the child: "Eat! Eat! Eat oh!" The elderly grandmother snatched the few packages: "Can't eat! Can't eat oh! It's, it's poisonous..."

Their whole hearts were stung. The two soldiers, like wounded beasts, retreated from the family.

Page 18

But tomorrow, they came again. ... In this way, they came here every day for a month. Now, the little girl was no longer afraid of them, and even called them uncles. The elderly grandmother also treated them very politely. She no longer greeted them with suspicious eyes. The two soldiers also seemed to feel very happy.

But one night, at about twelve o'clock in the middle of the night, gunshots suddenly rang out nearby. This dense and terrible sound continued for three hours before it finally subsided.

The next morning, everyone ran around telling each other: "The volunteers came yesterday!" "But they were defeated!" People sighed, and people were indignant. ...

This evening, the shorter soldier walked alone to the little girl's house. His face was all pale. He brought a bag of sweets. The old grandmother was very surprised and asked: "Where is the other one?"

"Killed last night!"

The whole room was filled with the silence of death. But it was still the elderly grandmother who spoke first: "I want to ask, why do you always bring us things to eat? You treat others very fiercely!"

"Alas: This child of yours is too much like my friend's child. We have been away from our hometown for several years, but we have never seen our wives and children at home. So when my friend saw your child, because she looked so much like them, he was so happy that he wanted to come here every day. - But, but now he's dead! Alas! What should his child do..."

"Who told you to come and beat us!" The old grandmother's angry words.

The shorter soldier silently slipped away during a period of silence!

Courtyard 202

— Liang Qiyun

The sunlight moved from the window to the top of the poplar tree, and gradually, it disappeared like a ghost. Then, the vast twilight melted away the light of day like flowing water.

The courtyard was quiet. Moreover, it had a somewhat desolate tone—next to the path paved with broken bricks, tangled weeds, wild vines, kudzu, and some similar climbing plants spread. Under the corner of the wall, several unknown purple small flowers drooped their heads. The haggard and sorrowful face of the poplar tree nailed them down. Not far from the foot of the tree, there was a pile of messy grass occupying a large area. A white kitten crawled out from there, paced to the shed at the entrance of the house, shook its body, and its golden, somewhat bewildered eyes suspiciously glanced around.

There was a time when this place was very lively, it was summer, right, every evening or night, people sat here, talking about things that it - the kitten - did not understand, but could be felt within its consciousness.

Maybe it was like this.

Young people often laughed, danced, and talked loudly about the charm of youth: middle-aged people came to chat about family affairs and human relationships: old people always sighed as their own comfort, because there were too many beautiful dreams in the past days. …

Later, I don't know why, people became deserted. Some just hid at home.

When a light breeze, turning from warm to slightly cold, slipped past, it just remembered to ask for news, but the cunning wind shook its head and left.

That day was a bright autumn day, and it felt excited. But, it didn't see people, where are the people?

In the afternoon, the sun gradually set in the west.

A little girl picked a large basket of wildflowers in the courtyard. It thought flowers were smart, so it went to ask the flowers. But, it was disappointed. - Other flowers were either taken to heaven by God, or they all wore haggard, tearful, bitter faces. Only those small flowers with fine yellow petals were in full bloom. However, seeing the pride and disregard for other things in those flowers, it hesitated.

It wanted to ask the grass, but the shrinking and declining appearance of the grass made it feel even more sad and sad.

-Why is it so lonely!

No answer, no reply. It was very annoyed…

A flock of crows returning to their nests, dragging mournful cries, swept across the sky. In the quiet twilight, fluctuating sounds floated.

Slowly - weakening: and quietly disappearing again.

The courtyard at dusk looked like it was tired and about to die.

Until dusk closed its gray, bewildered eyes and entered the realm of slumber, some dim lights shone through the windows from inside the house.

The light gently caressed the pale fabric of the small grass at the foot of the poplar tree. In this way, the old poplar tree sighed

-Why don't you also illuminate my haggard old face!

Perhaps it was bored, the white kitten crawled back into the pile of grass again.

The courtyard was always quiet. ……

Stage Play 204

Thunder and Lightning Drama Society

Suzhou Night Talk

Old painter Liu Shukang led four students to Suzhou to sketch, staying at the Suzhou Hotel. That morning, the teachers and students went to Tiger Hill for a pleasant outing. In the afternoon, male students A, B, C, and female student Yang Xiaofeng were chatting and laughing in the room, saying they were planning to go out to play and have tea, to see the women of Suzhou. Just as they were excitedly discussing and preparing to leave, the old painter suddenly appeared silently in the room. Seeing that the students only loved to fool around, and none of them were diligently painting, he immediately gave them a stern lecture. However, none of the male and female students wanted to listen to his theories and they all slipped away one by one! When he realized that there was no one in front of him listening to his art theory, he couldn't help but say with emotion, "Seeing the women of Suzhou" is much better than listening to an old man’s boring theories?

Suddenly, female student Xiaofeng turned back and, after asking why, realized that she couldn't go because her feet hurt from climbing the mountain in high heels that morning!

At this time, the old painter's hopes for his students were rekindled. He hoped that Xiaofeng could study painting well so that his art could be passed down. The clever Xiaofeng understood the old painter's intentions and recognized the old painter as her father because Xiaofeng's parents had already passed away.

The old painter was so happy he jumped up. The two went from being teacher and student to father and daughter. The old painter told Xiaofeng that he also used to have a lovely daughter who was lost during a warlord civil war. If she were still alive, she would be eighteen years old now! She was very smart since she was a child, and I remember teaching her four lines of Tang poetry when she was little: "Faintly, the long river flows; Leisurely, the traveler’s sentiment grows; Fallen flowers, though with regret, Fall to the earth without a sound." She learned it as soon as she heard it and sang it every day? Just as they were excitedly talking, a flower-selling girl suddenly ran in and interrupted their conversation! The old painter found it annoying and wanted to drive her out?

However, as the flower-selling girl was about to leave, she switched from the Suzhou dialect and recited the four lines of Tang poetry in the Beijing dialect: "Faintly, the long river flows; Leisurely, the traveler’s sentiment grows; Fallen flowers, though with regret, Fall to the earth without a sound." The old painter, touched by these four lines of Tang poetry, called her back and asked if she was from Beijing? And how she knew these four lines of Tang poetry. Who taught you? The flower girl told the old painter: "She used to have a painter father and a lovely mother. They lived in the suburbs of Beijing. That year, two warlords fought a civil war over territory, and their beautiful home was burned down by soldiers. Her father was said to have been burned to death at home. She and her mother could not survive in Beijing. Coincidentally, a fellow villager named Tang went to Suzhou to find her mother's sister, but the unfortunate are always unfortunate, and her mother's sister had already died! Of course, there was still no way to live, but thanks to the help of the Tang man, they managed to get by for a few more months. Later, the Tang man wanted her mother to marry him, promising to let her child study and receive education. Her mother, in order to fulfill her child's future happiness, sacrificed herself and married the Tang man. At first, the Tang man treated them well, but later, because her mother couldn't bear him a son, the Tang man took a concubine and abandoned them. Her mother, feeling deceived and sorry for her husband, became angry and died of illness. She is now a lonely girl who relies on selling flowers every day to support herself." Hearing this, the old painter knew that the flower girl was his lost daughter?

When the old painter told her that her father had not been burned to death by soldiers and that he was her father, the father and daughter hugged each other and cried. The daughter also told her father that her mother, when she was dying, still remembered her father's name and said she was sorry to him? At this time, Xiaofeng also knew that the flower girl was her sister.

Ballad Singing 207

Cai Xiaofang's Record of Retribution

Zhongxi (1040) 1:00 PM to 1:45 PM

Opening "Cries and Laughter Due to Greenery, Whipping Fengxi"

The general's angry eyes widened. Holding a rattan whip, he walked upstairs. Unexpectedly, I went to Tianjin yesterday for some business. You actually secretly sneaked out the door. Ah, you lowly person. One whip. One scold. He waved his hand and sent her away without stopping. All I saw was her snowy skin and cloud-like hair in disarray. Her clothes were untidy, revealing her chest. Fengxi heard. Trembling. Her whole body was covered in sweat. There are ears on the other side of the wall to prevent awareness. How could there be no eavesdroppers outside the window. Who would have thought that the angry general heard these words. He suddenly smiled coldly two or three times. I understand everything in your heart. Could it be that a secret rendezvous continues the old romance. I think you, living in a humble alley, are of lowly status. Singing and playing the clapperboard to make a living. Now you haven't changed your usual ways. I'm just afraid that the fox's tail is still alive and showing its shape. I thought you had changed your tune and disguised yourself as a student. Transforming into a dignified female student. Arrive here and enjoy prosperity. Rich clothes and jade food bring joy to your heart. Who knew that you were inherently a

Speaking of a way out, he also said that Mr. Wu Han had visited his home once a week after he was happily appointed as the section chief, meaning to introduce him to a position, but he politely declined. He said, "Mr. Wu Han, I will never forget this kindness."
